{BĀU, 1, 1}
uṣāḥ vai aśvasya medhyasya śiraḥ sūryaḥ cakṣuḥ vātaḥ prāṇaḥ vyāttam agniḥ vaiśvānaraḥ | [BĀU, 1, 1 561588_1]
saṃvatsaraḥ ātmā aśvasya medhyasya dyauḥ pṛṣṭham antarikṣam udaram pṛthivī pājasyam diśaḥ pārśve avāntaradiśaḥ parśavaḥ ṛtavaḥ aṅgāni māsāḥ ca ardha māsāḥ ca parvāṇi ahorātrāṇi pratiṣṭhā nakṣatrāṇi asthīni nabhaḥ māṃsāni ūvadhyam sikatāḥ sindhavaḥ gudāḥ yakṛt ca klomānaḥ ca parvatāḥ oṣadhayaḥ ca vanaspatayaḥ ca lomāni udyan pūrva ardhaḥ nimlocan jaghana ardhaḥ | [BĀU, 1, 1 561589_1]
yat vijṛmbhate tat vidyotate | [BĀU, 1, 1 561593_1]
yat vidhūnute tat stanayati | [BĀU, 1, 1 561594_1]
yat mehati tat varṣati | [BĀU, 1, 1 561595_1]
vāc eva asya vāc | [BĀU, 1, 1 561596_1]
ahar vai aśvam purastāt mahimā anvajāyata | [BĀU, 1, 1 561597_1]
tasya pūrve samudre yoniḥ | [BĀU, 1, 1 561598_1]
rātriḥ enam paścāt mahimā anvajāyata | [BĀU, 1, 1 561599_1]
tasya apare samudre yoniḥ | [BĀU, 1, 1 561600_1]
etau vai aśvam mahimnau abhitas saṃbabhūvatuḥ | [BĀU, 1, 1 561601_1]
hayaḥ bhūtvā devān avahat vājī gandharvān arvā asurān aśvaḥ manuṣyān | [BĀU, 1, 1 561602_1]
samudraḥ eva asya bandhuḥ samudraḥ yoniḥ | [BĀU, 1, 1 561603_1]

anantam vai manaḥ anantāḥ viśvāḥ devāḥ | [BĀU, 3, 1 562587_1]
anantam eva saḥ tena lokam jayati | [BĀU, 3, 1 562588_1]

tisraḥ iti | [BĀU, 3, 1 562590_1]

puronuvākyā ca yājyā ca | [BĀU, 3, 1 562592_1]

{BĀU, 3, 2}
atha hainaṃ jāratkārava ārtabhāgaḥ papraccha | [BĀU, 3, 2 1.1]
yājñavalkyeti hovāca kati grahāḥ katy atigrahā iti | [BĀU, 3, 2 1.2]
aṣṭau grahā aṣṭāv atigrahā iti | [BĀU, 3, 2 1.3]
ye te 'ṣṭau grahā aṣṭāv atigrahāḥ katame ta iti | [BĀU, 3, 2 1.4]
prāṇo vai grahaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 2.1]
so 'pānenātigraheṇa gṛhītaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 2.2]
prāṇena hi gandhāñ jighrati | [BĀU, 3, 2 2.3]
vāg vai grahaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 3.1]
sa nāmnātigraheṇa gṛhītaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 3.2]
vācā hi nāmāny abhivadati | [BĀU, 3, 2 3.3]
jihvā vai grahaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 4.1]
sa rasenātigraheṇa gṛhītaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 4.2]
jihvayā hi rasān vijānāti | [BĀU, 3, 2 4.3]
cakṣur vai grahaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 5.1]
sa rūpeṇātigraheṇa gṛhītaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 5.2]
cakṣuṣā hi rūpāṇi paśyati | [BĀU, 3, 2 5.3]
śrotraṃ vai grahaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 6.1]
sa śabdenātigraheṇa gṛhītaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 6.2]
śrotreṇa hi śabdāñ śṛṇoti | [BĀU, 3, 2 6.3]
mano vai grahaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 7.1]
sa kāmenātigraheṇa gṛhītaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 7.2]
manasā hi kāmān kāmayate | [BĀU, 3, 2 7.3]
hastau vai grahaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 8.1]
sa karmaṇātigraheṇa gṛhītaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 8.2]
hastābhyāṃ hi karma karoti | [BĀU, 3, 2 8.3]
tvag vai grahaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 9.1]
sa sparśenātigraheṇa gṛhītaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 9.2]
tvacā hi sparśān vedayate | [BĀU, 3, 2 9.3]
ity aṣṭau grahā aṣṭāv atigrahāḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 9.4]
yājñavalkyeti hovāca yad idaṃ sarvaṃ mṛtyor annaṃ kā svit sā devatā yasyā mṛtyur annam iti | [BĀU, 3, 2 10.1]
agnir vai mṛtyuḥ so 'pām annam | [BĀU, 3, 2 10.2]
apa punarmṛtyuṃ jayati | [BĀU, 3, 2 10.3]
yājñavalkyeti hovāca yatrāyaṃ puruṣo mriyata ud asmāt prāṇāḥ krāmanty āho neti | [BĀU, 3, 2 11.1]
neti hovāca yājñavalkyaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 11.2]
atraiva samavanīyante | [BĀU, 3, 2 11.3]
sa ucchvayati | [BĀU, 3, 2 11.4]
ādhmāyati | [BĀU, 3, 2 11.5]
ādhmāto mṛtaḥ śete | [BĀU, 3, 2 11.6]
yājñavalkyeti hovāca yatrāyaṃ puruṣo mriyate kim enaṃ na jahātīti | [BĀU, 3, 2 12.1]
nāmeti | [BĀU, 3, 2 12.2]
anantaṃ vai nāmānantā viśve devāḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 12.3]
anantam eva sa tena lokaṃ jayati | [BĀU, 3, 2 12.4]
yājñavalkyeti hovāca yatrāsya puruṣasya mṛtasyāgniṃ vāg apyeti vātaṃ prāṇaś cakṣur ādityaṃ manaś candraṃ diśaḥ śrotraṃ pṛthivīṃ śarīram ākāśam ātmauṣadhīr lomāni vanaspatīn keśā apsu lohitaṃ ca retaś ca nidhīyate kvāyaṃ tadā puruṣo bhavatīti | [BĀU, 3, 2 13.1]
āhara saumya hastam ārtabhāga | [BĀU, 3, 2 13.2]
āvām evaitasya vediṣyāvo na nāv etat sajana iti | [BĀU, 3, 2 13.3]
tau hotkramya mantrayāṃcakrāte | [BĀU, 3, 2 13.4]
tau ha yad ūcatuḥ karma haiva tad ūcatuḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 13.5]
atha ha yat praśaśaṃsatuḥ karma haiva tat praśaśaṃsatuḥ | [BĀU, 3, 2 13.6]
puṇyo vai puṇyena karmaṇā bhavati pāpaḥ pāpeneti | [BĀU, 3, 2 13.7]
tato ha jāratkārava ārtabhāga upararāma | [BĀU, 3, 2 13.8]
{BĀU, 3, 3}
atha hainaṃ bhujyur lāhyāyaniḥ papraccha yājñavalkyeti hovāca madreṣu carakāḥ paryavrajāma | [BĀU, 3, 3 1.1]
te patañcalasya kāpyasya gṛhān aima | [BĀU, 3, 3 1.2]
tasyāsīd duhitā gandharvagṛhītā | [BĀU, 3, 3 1.3]
tam apṛcchāma ko 'sīti | [BĀU, 3, 3 1.4]
so 'bravīt sudhanvāṅgirasa iti | [BĀU, 3, 3 1.5]
taṃ yadā lokānām antān apṛcchāma athainam abrūma kva pārikṣitā abhavann iti | [BĀU, 3, 3 1.6]
kva pārikṣitā abhavan | [BĀU, 3, 3 1.7]
sa tvā pṛcchāmi yājñavalkya kva pārikṣitā abhavann iti | [BĀU, 3, 3 1.8]
sa hovāca | [BĀU, 3, 3 2.1]
uvāca vai saḥ | [BĀU, 3, 3 2.2]
agacchan vai te tad yatrāśvamedhayājino gacchantīti | [BĀU, 3, 3 2.3]
kva nv aśvamedhayājino gacchantīti | [BĀU, 3, 3 2.4]
dvātriṃśataṃ vai devarathāhnyāny ayaṃ lokaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 3 2.5]
taṃ samantaṃ pṛthivī dvistāvat paryeti | [BĀU, 3, 3 2.6]
tāṃ samantaṃ pṛthivīṃ dvistāvat samudraḥ paryeti | [BĀU, 3, 3 2.7]
tad yāvatī kṣurasya dhārā yāvad vā makṣikāyāḥ pattraṃ tāvān antareṇākāśaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 3 2.8]
tān indraḥ suparṇo bhūtvā vāyave prāyacchat | [BĀU, 3, 3 2.9]
tān vāyur ātmani dhitvā tatrāgamayad yatrāśvamedhayājino 'bhavann iti | [BĀU, 3, 3 2.10]
evam iva vai sa vāyum eva praśaśaṃsa tasmād vāyur eva vyaṣṭir vāyuḥ samaṣṭiḥ | [BĀU, 3, 3 2.11]
apa punarmṛtyuṃ jayati ya evaṃ veda | [BĀU, 3, 3 2.12]
tato ha bhujyur lāhyāyanir upararāma | [BĀU, 3, 3 2.13]
{BĀU, 3, 4}
atha hainam uṣastaś cākrāyaṇaḥ papraccha | [BĀU, 3, 4 1.1]
yājñavalkyeti hovāca yat sākṣād aparokṣād brahma ya ātmā sarvāntaras taṃ me vyācakṣveti | [BĀU, 3, 4 1.2]
eṣa ta ātmā sarvāntaraḥ | [BĀU, 3, 4 1.3]
yaḥ prāṇena prāṇiti sa ta ātmā sarvāntaraḥ | [BĀU, 3, 4 1.4]
yo 'pānenāpāniti sa ta ātmā sarvāntaraḥ | [BĀU, 3, 4 1.5]
yo vyānena vyaniti sa ta ātmā sarvāntaraḥ | [BĀU, 3, 4 1.6]
ya udānenodaniti sa ta ātmā sarvāntaraḥ | [BĀU, 3, 4 1.7]
eṣa ta ātmā sarvāntaraḥ | [BĀU, 3, 4 1.8]
sa hovācoṣastaś cākrāyaṇaḥ yathā vai brūyād asau gaur asāv aśva ity evam evaitad vyapadiṣṭaṃ bhavati | [BĀU, 3, 4 2.1]
yad eva sākṣād aparokṣād brahma ya ātmā sarvāntaras taṃ me vyācakṣveti | [BĀU, 3, 4 2.2]
eṣa ta ātmā sarvāntaraḥ | [BĀU, 3, 4 2.3]
katamo yājñavalkya sarvāntaraḥ | [BĀU, 3, 4 2.4]
na dṛṣṭer draṣṭāraṃ paśyeḥ | [BĀU, 3, 4 2.5]
na śruteḥ śrotāraṃ śṛṇuyāḥ | [BĀU, 3, 4 2.6]
na mater mantāraṃ manvīthāḥ | [BĀU, 3, 4 2.7]
na vijñāter vijñātāraṃ vijānīyāḥ | [BĀU, 3, 4 2.8]
eṣa ta ātmā sarvāntaraḥ | [BĀU, 3, 4 2.9]
ato 'nyad ārtam | [BĀU, 3, 4 2.10]
tato hoṣastaś cākrāyaṇa upararāma | [BĀU, 3, 4 2.11]
{BĀU, 3, 5}
atha ha enam kaholaḥ kauṣītakeyaḥ papraccha | [BĀU, 3, 5 562688_1]
yājñavalkyaiḥ iti ha uvāca yat eva sākṣāt aparokṣāt brahma yaḥ ātmā sarva antaraḥ tam me vyācakṣva iti | [BĀU, 3, 5 562688_2]
eṣa te ātmā sarva antaraḥ | [BĀU, 3, 5 562690_1]
katamaḥ yājñavalkyaiḥ sarva antaraḥ | [BĀU, 3, 5 562691_1]
yaḥ aśanāyā pipāse śokam moham jarām mṛtyum atyeti etam vai tam ātmānam viditvā brāhmaṇāḥ putra eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vitta eṣaṇāyāḥ ca loka eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vyutthāya atha bhikṣā caryam caranti | [BĀU, 3, 5 562693_1]
yā hi eva putra eṣaṇā sā vitta eṣaṇā | [BĀU, 3, 5 562694_1]
yā vitta eṣaṇā sā loka eṣaṇā | [BĀU, 3, 5 562694_2]
ubhe hi ete eṣaṇe eva bhavataḥ | [BĀU, 3, 5 562695_1]
tasmāt brāhmaṇaḥ pāṇḍityam nirvidya bālyena tiṣṭhāset | [BĀU, 3, 5 562696_1]
bālyam ca pāṇḍityam ca nirvidya atha muniḥ | [BĀU, 3, 5 562697_1]
amaunam ca maunam ca nirvidya atha brāhmaṇaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 5 562698_1]
sa brāhmaṇaḥ kena syād yena syāt tenedṛśa eva | [BĀU, 3, 5 1.12]
atas anyat ārtam | [BĀU, 3, 5 562700_1]
tatas ha kaholaḥ kauṣītakeyaḥ upararāma | [BĀU, 3, 5 562701_1]
{BĀU, 3, 6}
atha hainaṃ gārgī vācaknavī papraccha yājñavalkyeti hovāca | [BĀU, 3, 6 1.1]
yad idaṃ sarvam apsv otaṃ ca protaṃ ca kasmin nu khalv āpa otāś ca protāś ceti | [BĀU, 3, 6 1.2]

{BĀU, 3, 7}
athainam uddālaka āruṇiḥ papraccha yājñavalkyeti hovāca | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.1]
madreṣv avasāma patañcalasya kāpyasya gṛheṣu yajñam adhīyānāḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.2]
tasyāsīd bhāryā gandharvagṛhītā | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.3]
tam apṛcchāma ko 'sīti | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.4]
so 'bravīt kabandha ātharvaṇa iti | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.5]
so 'bravīt patañcalaṃ kāpyaṃ yājñikāṃś ca vettha nu tvaṃ kāpya tat sūtraṃ yasminn ayaṃ ca lokaḥ paraś ca lokaḥ sarvāṇi ca bhūtāni saṃdṛbdhāni bhavantīti | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.6]
so 'bravīt patañcalaḥ kāpyo nāhaṃ tad bhagavan vedeti | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.7]
so 'bravīt patañcalaṃ kāpyaṃ yājñikāṃś ca | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.8]
vettha nu tvaṃ kāpya tam antaryāmiṇaṃ ya imaṃ ca lokaṃ paraṃ ca lokaṃ sarvāṇi ca bhūtāny antaro yamayati | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.9]
so 'bravīt patañcalaḥ kāpyo nāhaṃ taṃ bhagavan vedeti | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.10]
so 'bravīt patañcalaṃ kāpyaṃ yājñikāṃś ca | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.11]
yo vai tat kāpya sūtraṃ vidyāt taṃ cāntaryāmiṇam iti sa brahmavit sa lokavit sa devavit sa vedavit sa ātmavit sa sarvavit | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.12]
iti tebhyo 'bravīt | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.13]
tad ahaṃ veda | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.14]
tac cet tvaṃ yājñavalkya sūtram avidvāṃs taṃ cāntaryāmiṇaṃ brahmagavīr udajase mūrdhā te vipatiṣyati | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.15]
veda vā ahaṃ gautama tat sūtraṃ taṃ cāntaryāmiṇam iti | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.16]
yo vā idaṃ kaśca brūyād veda vedeti yathā vettha tathā brūhīti | [BĀU, 3, 7 1.17]
sa hovāca vāyur vai gautama tat sūtram | [BĀU, 3, 7 2.1]
vāyunā vai gautama sūtreṇāyaṃ ca lokaḥ paraś ca lokaḥ sarvāṇi ca bhūtāni saṃdṛbdhāni bhavanti | [BĀU, 3, 7 2.2]
tasmād vai gautama puruṣaṃ pretam āhur vyasraṃsiṣatāsyāṅgānīti | [BĀU, 3, 7 2.3]
vāyunā hi gautama sūtreṇa saṃdṛbdhāni bhavantīti | [BĀU, 3, 7 2.4]
evam evaitad yājñavalkya | [BĀU, 3, 7 2.5]
antaryāmiṇaṃ brūhīti | [BĀU, 3, 7 2.6]
yaḥ pṛthivyāṃ tiṣṭhan pṛthivyā antaro yaṃ pṛthivī na veda yasya pṛthivī śarīraṃ yaḥ pṛthivīm antaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 3.1]
yo 'psu tiṣṭhann adbhyo 'ntaro yam āpo na vidur yasyāpaḥ śarīraṃ yo 'po 'ntaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 4.1]
yo 'gnau tiṣṭhann agner antaro yam agnir na veda yasyāgniḥ śarīraṃ yo 'gnim antaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 5.1]
yo 'ntarikṣe tiṣṭhann antarikṣād antaro yam antarikṣaṃ na veda yasyāntarikṣaṃ śarīraṃ yo 'ntarikṣam antaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 6.1]
yo vāyau tiṣṭhan vāyor antaro yaṃ vāyur na veda yasya vāyuḥ śarīraṃ yo vāyum antaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 7.1]
yo divi tiṣṭhan divo 'ntaro yaṃ dyaur na veda yasya dyauḥ śarīraṃ yo divam antaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 8.1]
ya āditye tiṣṭhann ādityād antaro yam ādityo na veda yasyādityaḥ śarīraṃ ya ādityam antaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 9.1]
yo dikṣu tiṣṭhan digbhyo 'ntaro yaṃ diśo na vidur yasya diśaḥ śarīraṃ yo diśo 'ntaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 10.1]
yaś candratārake tiṣṭhaṃścandratārakād antaro yaṃ candratārakaṃ na veda yasya candratārakaṃ śarīraṃ yaś candratārakam antaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 11.1]
ya ākāśe tiṣṭhann ākāśād antaro yam ākāśo na veda yasyākāśaḥ śarīraṃ ya ākāśam antaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 12.1]
yas tamasi tiṣṭhaṃs tamaso 'ntaro yaṃ tamo na veda yasya tamaḥ śarīraṃ yas tamo 'ntaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 13.1]
yas tejasi tiṣṭhaṃs tejaso 'ntaro yaṃ tejo na veda yasya tejaḥ śarīraṃ yas tejo 'ntaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 14.1]
athādhibhūtam | [BĀU, 3, 7 15.1]
yaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu tiṣṭhan sarvebhyo bhūtebhyo 'ntaro yaṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāni na vidur yasya sarvāṇi bhūtāni śarīraṃ yaḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāny antaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 15.2]
ity adhibhūtam | [BĀU, 3, 7 15.3]
athādhyātmam | [BĀU, 3, 7 16.1]
yaḥ prāṇe tiṣṭhan prāṇād antaro yaṃ prāṇo na veda yasya prāṇaḥ śarīraṃ yaḥ prāṇam antaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 16.2]
yo vāci tiṣṭhan vāco 'ntaro yaṃ vāṅ na veda yasya vāk śarīraṃ yo vācam antaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 17.1]
yaś cakṣuṣi tiṣṭhaṃścakṣuṣo 'ntaro yaṃ cakṣur na veda yasya cakṣuḥ śarīraṃ yaś cakṣur antaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 18.1]
yaḥ śrotre tiṣṭhañchrotrād antaro yaṃ śrotraṃ na veda yasya śrotraṃ śarīraṃ yaḥ śrotram antaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 19.1]
yo manasi tiṣṭhan manaso 'ntaro yaṃ mano na veda yasya manaḥ śarīraṃ yo mano 'ntaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 20.1]
yas tvaci tiṣṭhaṃs tvaco 'ntaro yaṃ tvaṅ na veda yasya tvak śarīraṃ yas tvacam antaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 21.1]
yo vijñāne tiṣṭhan vijñānād antaro yaṃ vijñānaṃ na veda yasya vijñānaṃ śarīraṃ yo vijñānam antaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 22.1]
yo retasi tiṣṭhan retaso 'ntaro yaṃ reto na veda yasya retaḥ śarīraṃ yo reto 'ntaro yamayaty eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 23.1]
adṛṣṭo draṣṭāśrutaḥ śrotāmato mantāvijñāto vijñātā | [BĀU, 3, 7 23.2]
nānyo 'to 'sti draṣṭā nānyo 'to 'sti śrotā nānyo 'to 'sti mantā nānyo 'to 'sti vijñātā | [BĀU, 3, 7 23.3]
eṣa ta ātmāntaryāmy amṛtaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 7 23.4]
ato 'nyad ārtam | [BĀU, 3, 7 23.5]
tato hoddālaka āruṇir upararāma | [BĀU, 3, 7 23.6]
{BĀU, 3, 8}
atha ha vācaknavī uvāca brāhmaṇāḥ bhagavantaḥ _ aham imam dvau praśnau prakṣyāmi tau _ mama vivakṣyati na vai jātu vaḥ imam kaścid brahmodyam jetā iti | [BĀU, 3, 8 562781_1]
pṛccha gārgi iti | [BĀU, 3, 8 562784_1]
sā hovāca ahaṃ vai tvā yājñavalkya yathā kāśyo vā vaideho vograputra ujjyaṃ dhanur adhijyaṃ kṛtvā dvau bāṇavantau sapatnātivyādhinau haste kṛtvopottiṣṭhed evam evāhaṃ tvā dvābhyāṃ praśnābhyām upodasthām | [BĀU, 3, 8 2.1]
tau me brūhīti | [BĀU, 3, 8 2.2]
pṛccha gārgīti | [BĀU, 3, 8 2.3]
sā hovāca yad ūrdhvaṃ yājñavalkya divo yad avāk pṛthivyā yadantarā dyāvāpṛthivī ime yad bhūtaṃ ca bhavac ca bhaviṣyac cety ācakṣate kasmiṃs tad otaṃ ca protaṃ ceti | [BĀU, 3, 8 3.1]
sa hovāca yad ūrdhvaṃ gārgi divo yad avāk pṛthivyā yad antarā dyāvāpṛthivī ime yad bhūtaṃ ca bhavac ca bhaviṣyac cety ācakṣata ākāśe tad otaṃ ca protaṃ ceti | [BĀU, 3, 8 4.1]
sā hovāca namas te 'stu yājñavalkya yo ma etaṃ vyavoco 'parasmai dhārayasveti pṛccha gārgīti | [BĀU, 3, 8 5.1]
sā hovāca yad ūrdhvaṃ yājñavalkya divo yad avāk pṛthivyā yad antarā dyāvāpṛthivī ime yad bhūtaṃ ca bhavac ca bhaviṣyac cety ācakṣate kasmiṃs tad otaṃ ca protaṃ ceti | [BĀU, 3, 8 6.1]
sa hovāca yad ūrdhvaṃ gārgi divo yad avāk pṛthivyā yad antarā dyāvāpṛthivī ime yad bhūtaṃ ca bhavac ca bhaviṣyac cety ācakṣata ākāśa eva tad otaṃ ca protaṃ ceti | [BĀU, 3, 8 7.1]
kasmin nu khalv ākāśa otaś ca protaś ceti | [BĀU, 3, 8 7.2]
sa hovāca etad vai tad akṣaraṃ gārgi brāhmaṇā abhivadanty asthūlam anaṇv ahrasvam adīrgham alohitam asneham acchāyam atamo 'vāyv anākāśam asaṅgam arasam agandham acakṣuṣkam aśrotram avāg amano 'tejaskam aprāṇam amukham agātram anantaram abāhyam | [BĀU, 3, 8 8.1]
na tad aśnāti kiṃcana | [BĀU, 3, 8 8.2]
na tad aśnāti kaścana | [BĀU, 3, 8 8.3]
etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi sūryacandramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ | [BĀU, 3, 8 9.1]
etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi dyāvāpṛthivyau vidhṛte tiṣṭhataḥ | [BĀU, 3, 8 9.2]
etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi nimeṣā muhūrtā ahorātrāṇy ardhamāsā māsā ṛtavaḥ saṃvatsarā iti vidhṛtās tiṣṭhanti | [BĀU, 3, 8 9.3]
etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi prācyo 'nyā nadyaḥ syandante śvetebhyaḥ parvatebhyaḥ pratīcyo 'nyā yāṃ yāṃ ca diśam anu | [BĀU, 3, 8 9.4]
etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi manuṣyāḥ praśaṃsanti yajamānaṃ devā darvīṃ pitaro 'nvāyattāḥ | [BĀU, 3, 8 9.5]
yo vā etad akṣaram gārgy aviditvāsmiṃlloke juhoti yajate tapas tapyate bahūni varṣasahasrāṇy antavad evāsya tad bhavati | [BĀU, 3, 8 10.1]
yo vā etad akṣaram aviditvā gārgy aviditvāsmāllokāt praiti sa kṛpaṇaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 8 10.2]
atha ya etad akṣaraṃ gārgi viditvāsmāl lokāt praiti sa brāhmaṇaḥ | [BĀU, 3, 8 10.3]
tad vā etad akṣaraṃ gārgy adṛṣṭaṃ draṣṭraśrutaṃ śrotramataṃ mantravijñātaṃ vijñātṛ | [BĀU, 3, 8 11.1]
nānyad ato 'sti draṣṭṛ | [BĀU, 3, 8 11.2]
nānyad ato 'sti śrotṛ | [BĀU, 3, 8 11.3]
nānyad ato 'sti mantṛ | [BĀU, 3, 8 11.4]
nānyad ato 'sti vijñātṛ | [BĀU, 3, 8 11.5]
etasmin nu khalv akṣare gārgy ākāśa otaś ca protaś ca | [BĀU, 3, 8 11.6]
sā hovāca brāhmaṇā bhagavantas tad eva bahu manyadhvaṃ yad asmānnamaskāreṇa mucyedhvam | [BĀU, 3, 8 12.1]
na vai jātu yuṣmākam imaṃ kaścid brahmodyaṃ jeteti | [BĀU, 3, 8 12.2]
tato ha vācaknavy upararāma | [BĀU, 3, 8 12.3]

ādityajyotiḥ samrāḍ iti hovāca | [BĀU, 4, 3 2.2]
ādityenaivāyaṃ jyotiṣāste palyayate karma kurute vipalyetīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 2.3]
evam evaitad yājñavalkya | [BĀU, 4, 3 2.4]
astamita āditye yājñavalkya kiṃjyotir evāyaṃ puruṣa iti | [BĀU, 4, 3 3.1]
candramā evāsya jyotir bhavatīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 3.2]
candramasaivāyaṃ jyotiṣāste palyayate karma kurute vipalyetīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 3.3]
evam evaitad yājñavalkya | [BĀU, 4, 3 3.4]
astamita āditye yājñavalkya candramasy astamite kiṃjyotir evāyaṃ puruṣa iti | [BĀU, 4, 3 4.1]
agnir evāsya jyotir bhavatīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 4.2]
agninaiva jyotiṣāste palyayate karma kurute vipalyetīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 4.3]
evam evaitad yājñavalkya | [BĀU, 4, 3 4.4]
astamita āditye yājñavalkya candramasy astamite śānte 'gnau kiṃjyotir evāyaṃ puruṣa iti | [BĀU, 4, 3 5.1]
vāg evāsya jyotir bhavatīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 5.2]
vācaivāyaṃ jyotiṣāste palyayate karma kurute vipalyeti | [BĀU, 4, 3 5.3]
tasmād vai samrāḍ api yatra svaḥ pāṇir na vinirjñāyate 'tha yatra vāg uccaraty upaiva tatra nyetīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 5.4]
evam evaitad yājñavalkya | [BĀU, 4, 3 5.5]
astamita āditye yājñavalkya candramasy astamite śānte 'gnau śāntāyāṃ vāci kiṃjyotir evāyaṃ puruṣa iti | [BĀU, 4, 3 6.1]
ātmaivāsya jyotir bhavatīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 6.2]
ātmanaivāyaṃ jyotiṣāste palyayate karma kurute vipalyetīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 6.3]
katama ātmeti yo 'yaṃ vijñānamayaḥ prāṇeṣu hṛdy antarjyotiḥ puruṣaḥ sa samānaḥ sann ubhau lokāv anusaṃcarati dhyāyatīva lelāyatīva | [BĀU, 4, 3 7.1]
sa hi svapno bhūtvemaṃ lokam atikrāmati mṛtyo rūpāṇi | [BĀU, 4, 3 7.2]
sa vā ayaṃ puruṣo jāyamānaḥ śarīram abhisaṃpadyamānaḥ pāpmabhiḥ saṃsṛjyate | [BĀU, 4, 3 8.1]
sa utkrāman mriyamāṇaḥ pāpmano vijahāti | [BĀU, 4, 3 8.2]
tasya vā etasya puruṣasya dve eva sthāne bhavataḥ idaṃ ca paralokasthānaṃ ca | [BĀU, 4, 3 9.1]
saṃdhyaṃ tṛtīyaṃ svapnasthānam | [BĀU, 4, 3 9.2]
tasmin saṃdhye sthāne tiṣṭhan ubhe sthāne paśyatīdaṃ ca paralokasthānaṃ ca | [BĀU, 4, 3 9.3]
atha yathākramo 'yaṃ paralokasthāne bhavati tam ākramam ākramyobhayān pāpmana ānandāṃś ca paśyati | [BĀU, 4, 3 9.4]
sa yatra prasvapity asya lokasya sarvāvato mātrām apādāya svayaṃ vihatya svayaṃ nirmāya svena bhāsā svena jyotiṣā prasvapiti | [BĀU, 4, 3 9.5]
atrāyaṃ puruṣaḥ svayaṃjyotir bhavati | [BĀU, 4, 3 9.6]
na tatra rathā na rathayogā na panthāno bhavanti | [BĀU, 4, 3 10.1]
atha rathān rathayogān pathaḥ sṛjate | [BĀU, 4, 3 10.2]
na tatrānandā mudaḥ pramudo bhavanti | [BĀU, 4, 3 10.3]
athānandān mudaḥ pramudaḥ sṛjate | [BĀU, 4, 3 10.4]
na tatra veśāntāḥ puṣkariṇyaḥ sravantyo bhavanti | [BĀU, 4, 3 10.5]
atha veśāntān puṣkariṇīḥ sravantīḥ sṛjate | [BĀU, 4, 3 10.6]
sa hi kartā | [BĀU, 4, 3 10.7]
tad ete ślokā bhavanti | [BĀU, 4, 3 11.1]
svapnena śārīram abhiprahatyāsuptaḥ suptān abhicākaśīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 11.2]
śukram ādāya punar aiti sthānaṃ hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣa ekahaṃsaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 11.3]
prāṇena rakṣann avaraṃ kulāyaṃ bahiṣkulāyād amṛtaś caritvā | [BĀU, 4, 3 12.1]
sa īyate 'mṛto yatrakāmaṃ hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣa ekahaṃsaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 12.2]
svapnānta uccāvacam īyamāno rūpāṇi devaḥ kurute bahūni | [BĀU, 4, 3 13.1]
uteva strībhiḥ saha modamāno jakṣad utevāpi bhayāni paśyan | [BĀU, 4, 3 13.2]
ārāmam asya paśyanti na taṃ paśyati kaścaneti | [BĀU, 4, 3 14.1]
taṃ nāyataṃ bodhayed ity āhuḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 14.2]
durbhiṣajyaṃ hāsmai bhavati yam eṣa na pratipadyate | [BĀU, 4, 3 14.3]
atho khalv āhur jāgaritadeśa evāsyaiṣa iti | [BĀU, 4, 3 14.4]
yāni hy eva jāgrat paśyati tāni supta iti | [BĀU, 4, 3 14.5]
atrāyaṃ puruṣaḥ svayaṃjyotir bhavati | [BĀU, 4, 3 14.6]
so 'haṃ bhagavate sahasraṃ dadāmi | [BĀU, 4, 3 14.7]
ata ūrdhvaṃ vimokṣāya brūhīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 14.8]
sa vā eṣa etasmin saṃprasāde ratvā caritvā dṛṣṭvaiva puṇyaṃ ca pāpaṃ ca punaḥ pratinyāyaṃ pratiyony ādravati svapnāyaiva | [BĀU, 4, 3 15.1]
sa yat tatra kiṃcit paśyaty ananvāgatas tena bhavati | [BĀU, 4, 3 15.2]
asaṅgo hy ayaṃ puruṣa iti | [BĀU, 4, 3 15.3]
evam evaitat yājñavalkya | [BĀU, 4, 3 15.4]
so 'haṃ bhagavate sahasraṃ dadāmi | [BĀU, 4, 3 15.5]
ata ūrdhvaṃ vimokṣāyaiva brūhīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 15.6]
sa vā eṣa etasmin svapne ratvā caritvā dṛṣṭvaiva puṇyaṃ ca pāpaṃ ca punaḥ pratinyāyaṃ pratiyony ādravati buddhāntāyaiva | [BĀU, 4, 3 16.1]
sa yat tatra kiṃcit paśyaty ananvāgatas tena bhavati | [BĀU, 4, 3 16.2]
asaṅgo hy ayaṃ puruṣa iti | [BĀU, 4, 3 16.3]
evam evaitat yājñavalkya | [BĀU, 4, 3 16.4]
so 'haṃ bhagavate sahasraṃ dadāmi | [BĀU, 4, 3 16.5]
ata ūrdhvaṃ vimokṣāyaiva brūhīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 16.6]
sa vā eṣa etasmin buddhānte ratvā caritvā dṛṣṭvaiva puṇyaṃ ca pāpaṃ ca punaḥ pratinyāyaṃ pratiyony ādravati svapnāntāyaiva | [BĀU, 4, 3 17.1]
tad yathā mahāmatsya ubhe kūle anusaṃcarati pūrvaṃ cāparaṃ ca evam evāyaṃ puruṣa etāv ubhāv antāv anusaṃcarati svapnāntaṃ ca buddhāntaṃ ca | [BĀU, 4, 3 18]
tad yathāsminn ākāśe śyeno vā suparṇo vā viparipatya śrāntaḥ saṃhatya pakṣau saṃlayāyaiva dhriyate evam evāyaṃ puruṣa etasmā antāya dhāvati yatra supto na kaṃcana kāmaṃ kāmayate na kaṃcana svapnaṃ paśyati | [BĀU, 4, 3 19]
tā vā asyaitā hitā nāma nāḍyo yathā keśaḥ sahasradhā bhinnas tāvatāṇimnā tiṣṭhanti śuklasya nīlasya piṅgalasya haritasya lohitasya pūrṇāḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 20.1]
atha yatrainaṃ ghnantīva jinantīva hastīva vicchāyayati gartam iva patati yad eva jāgrad bhayaṃ paśyati tad atrāvidyayā manyate | [BĀU, 4, 3 20.2]
atha yatra deva iva rājevāham evedaṃ sarvo 'smīti manyate so 'sya paramo lokaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 20.3]
tad vā asyaitad aticchando 'pahatapāpmābhayaṃ rūpam | [BĀU, 4, 3 21.1]
tad yathā priyayā striyā sampariṣvakto na bāhyaṃ kiṃcana veda nāntaram evam evāyaṃ puruṣaḥ prājñenātmanā sampariṣvakto na bāhyaṃ kiṃcana veda nāntaram | [BĀU, 4, 3 21.2]
tad vā asyaitad āptakāmam ātmakāmam akāmaṃ rūpam śokāntaram | [BĀU, 4, 3 21.3]
atra pitāpitā bhavati mātāmātā lokā alokā devā adevā vedā avedāḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 22.1]
atra steno 'steno bhavati bhrūṇahābhrūṇahā cāṇḍālo 'caṇḍālaḥ paulkaso 'paulkasaḥ śramaṇo 'śramaṇas tāpaso 'tāpasaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 22.2]
ananvāgataṃ puṇyenānanvāgataṃ pāpena | [BĀU, 4, 3 22.3]
tīrṇo hi tadā sarvāñ śokān hṛdayasya bhavati | [BĀU, 4, 3 22.4]
yad vai tan na paśyati paśyan vai tan na paśyati | [BĀU, 4, 3 23.1]
na hi draṣṭur dṛṣṭer viparilopo vidyate 'vināśitvāt | [BĀU, 4, 3 23.2]
na tu tad dvitīyam asti tato 'nyad vibhaktaṃ yat paśyet | [BĀU, 4, 3 23.3]
yad vai tan na jighrati jighran vai tan na jighrati | [BĀU, 4, 3 24.1]
na hi ghrātur ghrāter viparilopo vidyate 'vināśitvāt | [BĀU, 4, 3 24.2]
na tu tad dvitīyam asti tato 'nyad vibhaktaṃ yaj jighret | [BĀU, 4, 3 24.3]
yad vai tan na rasayati rasayan vai tan na rasayati | [BĀU, 4, 3 25.1]
na hi rasayitū rasayater viparilopo vidyate 'vināśitvāt | [BĀU, 4, 3 25.2]
na tu tad dvitīyam asti tato 'nyad vibhaktaṃ yad rasayet | [BĀU, 4, 3 25.3]
yad vai tan na vadati vadan vai tan na vadati | [BĀU, 4, 3 26.1]
na hi vaktur vakter viparilopo vidyate 'vināśitvāt | [BĀU, 4, 3 26.2]
na tu tad dvitīyam asti tato 'nyad vibhaktaṃ yad vadet | [BĀU, 4, 3 26.3]
yad vai tan na śṛṇoti śṛṇvan vai tan na śṛṇoti | [BĀU, 4, 3 27.1]
na hi śrotuḥ śruter viparilopo vidyate 'vināśitvāt | [BĀU, 4, 3 27.2]
na tu tad dvitīyam asti tato 'nyad vibhaktaṃ yacchṛṇuyāt | [BĀU, 4, 3 27.3]
yad vai tan na manute manvāno vai tan na manute | [BĀU, 4, 3 28.1]
na hi mantur mater viparilopo vidyate 'vināśitvāt | [BĀU, 4, 3 28.2]
na tu tad dvitīyam asti tato 'nyad vibhaktaṃ yan manvīta | [BĀU, 4, 3 28.3]
yad vai tan na spṛśati spṛśan vai tan na spṛśati | [BĀU, 4, 3 29.1]

yatra vā anyad iva syāt tatrānyo 'nyat paśyed anyo 'nyaj jighred anyo 'nyad rasayed anyo 'nyad vaded anyo 'nyacchṛṇuyād anyo 'nyan manvītānyo 'nyat spṛśed anyo 'nyad vijānīyāt | [BĀU, 4, 3 31.1]
salila eko draṣṭādvaito bhavati | [BĀU, 4, 3 32.1]
eṣa brahmalokaḥ samrāṭ | [BĀU, 4, 3 32.2]

eṣāsya paramā gatiḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 32.4]
eṣāsya paramā saṃpat | [BĀU, 4, 3 32.5]
eṣo 'sya paramo lokaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 32.6]
eṣo 'sya parama ānandaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 32.7]
etasyaivānandasyānyāni bhūtāni mātrām upajīvanti | [BĀU, 4, 3 32.8]
sa yo manuṣyāṇāṃ rāddhaḥ samṛddho bhavaty anyeṣām adhipatiḥ sarvair mānuṣyakair bhogaiḥ sampannatamaḥ sa manuṣyāṇāṃ parama ānandaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.1]
atha ye śataṃ manuṣyāṇām ānandāḥ sa ekaḥ pitṝṇāṃ jitalokānām ānandaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.2]
atha ye śataṃ pitṝṇāṃ jitalokānām ānandāḥ sa eko gandharvaloka ānandaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.3]
atha ye śataṃ gandharvaloka ānandāḥ sa ekaḥ karmadevānām ānando ye karmaṇā devatvam abhisaṃpadyante | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.4]
atha ye śataṃ karmadevānām ānandāḥ sa eka ājānadevānām ānandaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.5]
yaś ca śrotriyo 'vṛjino 'kāmahataḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.6]
atha ye śatam ājānadevānām ānandāḥ sa ekaḥ prajāpatiloka ānandaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.7]
yaś ca śrotriyo 'vṛjino 'kāmahataḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.8]
atha ye śataṃ prajāpatiloka ānandāḥ sa eko brahmaloka ānandaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.9]
yaś ca śrotriyo 'vṛjino 'kāmahataḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.10]
athaiṣa eva parama ānandaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.11]
eṣa brahmalokaḥ samrāṭ | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.12]
iti hovāca yājñavalkyaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.13]
so 'haṃ bhagavate sahasraṃ dadāmi | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.14]
ata ūrdhvaṃ vimokṣāyaiva brūhīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.15]
atra ha yājñavalkyo bibhayāṃcakāra medhāvī rājā sarvebhyo māntebhya udarautsīd iti | [BĀU, 4, 3 33.16]
sa vā eṣa etasmin svapnānte ratvā caritvā dṛṣṭvaiva puṇyaṃ ca pāpaṃ ca punaḥ pratinyāyaṃ pratiyony ādravati buddhāntāyaiva | [BĀU, 4, 3 34.1]
tad yathānaḥ susamāhitam utsarjaṃ yāyād evam evāyaṃ śārīra ātmā prājñenātmanānvārūḍha utsarjaṃ yāti | [BĀU, 4, 3 35.1]
yatraitad ūrdhvocchvāsī bhavati | [BĀU, 4, 3 35.2]
sa yatrāyam aṇimānaṃ nyeti jarayā vopatapatā vāṇimānaṃ nigacchati | [BĀU, 4, 3 36.1]
tad yathāmraṃ vodumbaraṃ vā pippalaṃ vā bandhanāt pramucyate | [BĀU, 4, 3 36.2]
evam evāyaṃ puruṣa ebhyo 'ṅgebhyaḥ sampramucya punaḥ pratinyāyaṃ pratiyony ādravati prāṇāyaiva | [BĀU, 4, 3 36.3]
tad yathā rājānam āyantam ugrāḥ pratyenasaḥ sūtagrāmaṇyo 'nnaiḥ pānair avasathaiḥ pratikalpante 'yam āyāty ayam āgacchatīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 37.1]
evaṃ haivaṃvidaṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāni pratikalpanta idaṃ brahmāyātīdam āgacchatīti | [BĀU, 4, 3 37.2]

yatraitad ūrdhvocchvāsī bhavati | [BĀU, 4, 3 38.3]
{BĀU, 4, 4}
sa yatrāyam ātmābalyaṃ nyetya saṃmoham iva nyeti | [BĀU, 4, 4 1.1]
athainam ete prāṇā abhisamāyanti | [BĀU, 4, 4 1.2]
sa etās tejomātrāḥ samabhyādadāno hṛdayam evānvavakrāmati | [BĀU, 4, 4 1.3]
sa yatraiṣa cākṣuṣaḥ puruṣaḥ parāṅ paryāvartate | [BĀU, 4, 4 1.4]
athārūpajño bhavati | [BĀU, 4, 4 1.5]
ekībhavati na paśyatīty āhuḥ | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.1]
ekībhavati na jighratīty āhuḥ | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.2]
ekībhavati na rasayatīty āhuḥ | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.3]
ekībhavati na vadatīty āhuḥ | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.4]
ekībhavati na śṛṇotīty āhuḥ | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.5]
ekībhavati na manuta ity āhuḥ | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.6]
ekībhavati na spṛśatīty āhuḥ | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.7]
ekībhavati na vijānātīty āhuḥ | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.8]
tasya haitasya hṛdayasyāgraṃ pradyotate | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.9]
tena pradyotenaiṣa ātmā niṣkrāmati | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.10]
cakṣuṣṭo vā mūrdhno vānyebhyo vā śarīradeśebhyaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.11]
tam utkrāmantaṃ prāṇo 'nūtkrāmati | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.12]
prāṇam anūtkrāmantaṃ sarve prāṇā anūtkrāmanti | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.13]
savijñāno bhavati | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.14]
savijñānam evānvavakrāmati | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.15]
taṃ vidyākarmaṇī samanvārabhete pūrvaprajñā ca | [BĀU, 4, 4 2.16]
tad yathā tṛṇajalāyukā tṛṇasyāntaṃ gatvānyam ākramam ākramyātmānam upasaṃharati | [BĀU, 4, 4 3.1]
evam evāyam ātmedaṃ śarīraṃ nihatyāvidyāṃ gamayitvānyam ākramam ākramyātmānam upasaṃharati | [BĀU, 4, 4 3.2]
tad yathā peśaskārī peśaso mātrām apādāyānyan navataraṃ kalyāṇataraṃ rūpaṃ tanute | [BĀU, 4, 4 4.1]
evam evāyam ātmedaṃ śarīraṃ nihatyāvidyāṃ gamayitvānyan navataraṃ kalyāṇataraṃ rūpaṃ kurute | [BĀU, 4, 4 4.2]
pitryaṃ vā gāndharvaṃ vā daivaṃ vā prājāpatyaṃ vā brāhmaṃ vānyeṣāṃ vā bhūtānām | [BĀU, 4, 4 4.3]
sa vā ayam ātmā brahma vijñānamayo manomayo prāṇamayaś cakṣurmayaḥ śrotramayaḥ pṛthivīmaya āpomayo vāyumaya ākāśamayas tejomayo 'tejomayaḥ kāmamayo 'kāmamayaḥ krodhamayo 'krodhamayo dharmamayo 'dharmamayaḥ sarvamayaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 4 5.1]
tad yad etad idaṃmayo 'domaya iti | [BĀU, 4, 4 5.2]
yathākārī yathācārī tathā bhavati | [BĀU, 4, 4 5.3]
sādhukārī sādhur bhavati | [BĀU, 4, 4 5.4]
pāpakārī pāpo bhavati | [BĀU, 4, 4 5.5]
puṇyaḥ puṇyena karmaṇā pāpaḥ pāpena | [BĀU, 4, 4 5.6]
atho khalv āhuḥ | [BĀU, 4, 4 5.7]
kāmamaya evāyaṃ puruṣa iti | [BĀU, 4, 4 5.8]
sa yathākāmo bhavati tatkratur bhavati | [BĀU, 4, 4 5.9]
yatkratur bhavati tat karma kurute | [BĀU, 4, 4 5.10]
yat karma kurute tad abhisaṃpadyate | [BĀU, 4, 4 5.11]
tad eṣa śloko bhavati | [BĀU, 4, 4 6.1]
tad eva saktaḥ saha karmaṇaiti liṅgaṃ mano yatra niṣaktam asya | [BĀU, 4, 4 6.2]
prāpyāntaṃ karmaṇas tasya yat kiñceha karoty ayam | [BĀU, 4, 4 6.3]
tasmāllokāt punar aity asmai lokāya karmaṇe | [BĀU, 4, 4 6.4]
iti nu kāmayamānaḥ | [BĀU, 4, 4 6.5]

{BĀU, 6, 3}
sa yaḥ kāmayeta mahat prāpnuyām ity udagayana āpūryamāṇapakṣasya puṇyāhe dvādaśāham upasadvratī bhūtvaudumbare kaṃse camase vā sarvauṣadhaṃ phalānīti saṃbhṛtya parisamuhya parilipyāgnim upasamādhāya paristīryāvṛtājyaṃ saṃskṛtya puṃsā nakṣatreṇa manthaṃ saṃnīya juhoti | [BĀU, 6, 3 1.1]
yāvanto devās tvayi jātavedas tiryañco ghnanti puruṣasya kāmān | [BĀU, 6, 3 1.2]
tebhyo 'haṃ bhāgadheyaṃ juhomi te mā tṛptāḥ sarvaiḥ kāmais tarpayantu svāhā | [BĀU, 6, 3 1.3]
yā tiraścī nipadyase 'haṃ vidharaṇī iti | [BĀU, 6, 3 1.4]
